# VRD annotation customisation instructions file

# Step 11 of the annotations customisation process: apply further vr-specific
# changes and removals.

# Step 11 was introduced because the problems being fixed here were
# identified within the customised annotations produced after application
# of annotation customisation steps 1 through 10.  Given that so many
# annotation changes are applied during steps 1 through 10, it was felt it
# would be unsafe to extend/amend the customisations applied in steps 1
# through 10. Instead, it was deemed to be much safer to augment the
# annotation customisation process by adding this supplementary
# customisation step.

# The annotation customisation instructions specified here adhere to the
# same instruction protocol as used in all other instruction files.

# start of annotation customisation instructions
